 Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā sambuddhassa  
  
 Paṭhamo vaggo 
  
      
  
 Puggalakathā 
  
   Sakavādipucchā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti     
  
 Paravādipaṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Sakavādianuyogo yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho   Tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti     
  
 Paravādipaṭikkhepo nahevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 Sakavādiniggaho ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
      
  
   Sacchikaṭṭhaparamaṭṭhenāti   syā 
   Sacchikaṭṭho paramaṭṭho   syā 
  
                
  
 Anulomaṭhapanā hañcī puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anulomapāpanā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho   Tato so puggalo 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthoti  
 Anuloma āropanā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 Paṭilomaṭhapanā no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Paṭilomapāpana no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭiloma āropanā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 Anuloma pañcakaṃ  
  
   Paravādipucchā puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti    
  
 Sakavādipaṭiññā āmantā                  
 Paravādianuyogo yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭikkhepo nahevaṃ vattabbe  
 Paravādipaṭikammaṃ ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
  
        
  
   Saccikaṭṭho paramaṭṭho   syā 
   Sacchikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti   syā  
  
                
  
 Anulomaṭhapanā hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anulomapāpanā tena vata re vattabbe so saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Anuloma āropanā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 Paṭilomaṭhapanā no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭiloma āropanā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 Paṭikammacatukkaṃ 
  
   Pa Ni Tvaṃ ce pana maññasi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti tena tava tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ 
 paṭijānantaṃ hevaṃ niggahetabbe atha taṃ niggaṇhāmi Suniggahīto ca hosi  
  
 Anu ha hañci puggelo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭha paramatthena  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalonūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
                
  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā                  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Paṭi Ā Yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 Niggaha catukkaṃ  
  
   Pa U ese ce dunniggahite hevamevaṃ tattha dakkhā vattabbe kho puggaloupalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti No ca mayaṃ tayā tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ 
 paṭijānattā hevaṃ niggahetabbaṃ Atha maṃ niggaṇhāsi dunniggahitā ca homa  
  
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
                  
  
 Yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca 
 vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti 
 micchā  
  
 Pari ha no ca pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 Upanayanacakukkaṃ                  
  
   Pa Niga na hevaṃ niggahatabbe tena hi yaṃ niggaṇhāsi  
  
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 upalabbhati   Saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalouppalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      
   Nūpalabbhati  P T S   
  
                  
  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccakaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo uppalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 Nigamanaṃ tena hi ye kate niggahe se niggahe dukkaṭe sukate paṭikimme Sukata 
 paṭipādanāti 
  
 Nigamana   Catukkaṃ  
  
 Paṭhamo niggaho  
  
 Pa Pu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 Pa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 Anu ha hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalā nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo                 saccikaṭṭho 
 paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā 
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
       
  
   Niggamana   sīmu Machasaṃ  
  
                  
  
 No ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalababhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti Micchā  
  
 Paccanika pañcakaṃ  
  
   Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe 
 Sa Paṭikamma ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micachā Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho 
 paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe pugagalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 Paṭikammacatukkaṃ                  
                  
  
   Sa Ni Tvā ce pana maññasi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramatto tato so puggalo 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti tena tava tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ 
 paṭijānantaṃ hevaṃ niggahetabbe atha taṃ niggaṇhāmi Suniggahito ca hosi  
  
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggaloupalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 Niggaha catukkaṃ  
  
   Sa U ese ce dunniggahite hevamevaṃ tattha dakkha vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tatoso puggalo 
 nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti No ca mayaṃ tayā tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ 
 paṭijānantā hevaṃ niggahetabbā Atha maṃ niggaṇhāsi dunniggahitā ca homa  
  
                  
  
 Anu ha hañca puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭha paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati                  
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo 
 nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramatto tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikatthaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 Upanayana catukkaṃ 
  
    Sa Ni na hevaṃ niggahetabbe tena hi yaṃ niggaṇhāsi  
 Anu ha Hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re cattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati scacikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
                  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti 
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalaba bhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
 Nigamanaṃ tena hi ye kate niggahe se niggahe dukkaṭe Sukate paṭikamme Sukatā 
 paṭipādanāti  
  
 Nigamana catukkaṃ 
  
 Dutiyo niggaho                  
  
    Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa anu sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Avajānanā na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 Sa Ni Ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
                  
  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  pe  
  
 Tatiyo niggaho  
  
    Sa Pu Puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Pavi na havaṃ vattabbe  
 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparatthena no ca 
 vattabba sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe sabbadā                 puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  pe   
  
 Catuttho niggaho  
                  
  
 Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sabbesu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 Sa Ni ājanāhi niggahaṃ  
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sabbesu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca 
 vattabbe sabbosu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe sabbosu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbepuggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca 
 vattabbe sabbesu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  Pe  
  
 Pañcamo niggaho  
  
    Pa Pu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu sabbattha puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 Pa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 Anu ha hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
                  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sabbattha puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe sabbatta puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā      
              
 Paṭi ha No ce pana vattabbe sabbattha puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti 
 paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe sabbattha puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 Chaṭṭho niggaho 
  
    Pa Pu Puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu sabbadā puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 Pa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 Anu ha hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sabbadā puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe sabbadā puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
                  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe sabbadā puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe sabbadā puggalo nūpalababati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  Pe  
  
 Sattamo niggaho 
  
    Pa Pu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu sabbesu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe                   
 Pa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 Anu ha hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sabbesu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe sabbesu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe sabbesu puggalonūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi Vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no 
 ca vattabbe sabbesu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  pe  
  
 Aṭṭhamo niggaho 
  
                  
  
    Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti 
 Pa Paṭi hevaṃ vattabbe 
 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbeaññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi  Vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccakaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggalo ti 
 micchā  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe aññaraṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena                  no ca vattabbe 
 aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggalo ti micchā  pe  
  
         Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena vedanā ca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena   pe  saññā ca upalabbhati  pesaṅkārā ca upalabbhanti 
  peviññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
                  
  
 Sa Anu aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe 
 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ aññño puggaloti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño 
 puggalo ti micchā  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 viñññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño 
 puggalo ti micchā  pe  
  
    Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena cakkhāyatanañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  sotāyatanañca upalanabbhati   pe  ghānāyatanañca 
 upalabbhati  pe  jivhāyatanañca upalabbhati  pekāyāyatanañca upalabbhati  pe  
 rūpāyatanañca upalabbhati  pesaddāyatanañca upalabbati  pe  gandhāyatanañca upalabbhati 
  perasāyatanañca upalabbhati  pe  phoṭṭhabbāyatanañca upalabbhati  pemanāyatanañca 
 upalabbhati  pe  dhammāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
  
                  
  
         Sa Pu Cakkhudhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pesotadhātu ca 
 upalabbhati  pe  ghānadhātu ca upalabbhati  pejivhādhātu ca upalabbhati  pekāyadhātu ca 
 upalabbhati  perūpadhātu ca upalabbhati  pe  sadda dhātu ca upalabbhati  pegandhadhātu 
 ca upalabbhati  pe  rasadhātu ca upalabbhati  pephoṭṭhabbadhātu ca upalabbhati  pe   
  
 Sa Pu Cakkhuviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati  pe  sotaviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati 
  peghānaviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati  pejivhāviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati 
  pekāyaviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati  pe  manodhātu ca upalabbhati  pe  dhammadhātu ca 
 upalabbhati  pemanoviññāṇadhātu ca   Upalabbhati  pemanoviññāṇadhātu   ca 
 upalabbhati    Pesaccikaṭṭhaparamatthena                   
  Pe   
  
    Cakkhundriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pesotindriyañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  peghanindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
 kāyindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  manindriyañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pejīvitindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
 itthindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  purisindriyañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  sukhindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
 dukkhindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pesomanassindriyañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Sa Anu aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
        
   Manoviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati 
 sacchikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe machasaṃ sīmu syā  
  
                  
  
 Anu ha hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 Aññāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Sa Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ 
 aññātāvindriyaṃ aññopuggaloti micchā  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Paṭi Pā no ca pana vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ 
 aññātāvindriyaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  Pe   
  
    Pa Pu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Pa Pu vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno rūpañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Pa Anu aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Sa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe 
  
 Pa Paṭikammaṃ ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
  
                  
  
 Pa ha hañci vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno rūpañcupalababhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anu pā tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Anu ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya 
 paṭipanno rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño 
 puggaloti micchā                   
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Pa pā no ca vata re vattabbe vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno rūpañca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Pa ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno 
 rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti 
 micchā  pe  
    Pa Pu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Pa Pu vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno vedanā ca upalabbhati  pe  
 saññā ca upalabbhati  pe  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti  pe  viññāṇañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Pa Anu añññāṃ viññāṇaṃ aññe puggaloti  
  
 Sa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 Pa Paṭikammaṃ ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
  
                  
  
 Anu ṭha hañci vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno viññāṇañca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anu pā tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Anu ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya 
 paṭipanno viññānagñca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ 
 viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Pa Pā no ca vata re vattabbe vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthipuggalo attahitāya paṭipanno 
 viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Pa Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vatactabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya 
 paṭipanno viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ 
 viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  pe  
  
          Pa Pu puggalo nūupalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Pa Pu vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno cakkhāyatanañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  sotāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 dhammāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
  
 Cakakhudhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  kāyādhātu ca upalabbhati  pe  
 rūpadhātu ca upalabbhati  pe  phoṭṭhabbadhātu ca upalabbhati  pe  cakkhuviññāṇadhātu 
 ca upalabbhati  pe  manodhātu ca upalabbhati  pe  dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati 
  pemanoviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati    Saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
  
        Manoviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena machasaṃ sīmu syā  pe  
  
                  
 Cakkhundriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  sotindriyañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  aññindriyañca   Upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
  
     Pa Pu puggalo nūupalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti 
  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Pa Pu vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno aññātāvindriyañca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Pa Anu aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Sa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 Pa Paṭikammaṃ ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
  
 Anu ha hañci vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitaṃya paṭipanno aññātāvindriyañca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya 
 paṭipanno aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ 
 aññātāvindriyaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno 
 aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya 
 paṭipanno aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ 
 aññātāvindriyaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  pe  
  
 Suddhikasaṃsandanā  
  
   Aññātāvindriyañca   sīmu Syā  
  
                  
  
     Sa Pu rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena vedanā ca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññaṃ vedanāti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
  
 Sa Pucchā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Sa Anu aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Pa Paṭi Na hevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
 Anu ha hañci rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena vedanā ca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññā vedanā puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena vedanā 
 ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññā vedanā puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe 
 aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti micchā                   
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena vedanā ca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññā vedanā puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpaṃca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
                  
  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena vedanā 
 ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññā vedanā puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe 
 aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  pe  
  
          Sa Pu rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena saññā ca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññaṃ viññāṇanti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Sa Anu Aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabe  
  
 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
 Anu ha hañci rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ puggalo 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca 
 vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  
  
                  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ puggalo 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca 
 vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  Pe  
  
     Sa Pu vedanā upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena saññā ca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
 viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  rūpañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
  
 Saññā upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti  peviññāṇañca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
  pe  saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
  
 Saṅkhārā upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  vedanā 
 ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  saññā ca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  
  
 Sa Pu viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  saññāca 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño saṅkhārāti  Pe  añño saṅkhārāti  Pe  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
                  
  
 Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe                   
 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 Anu ha hañci viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño saṅkārā puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena palabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ aññe saṅkhārā 
 puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  
  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vanattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe viññāṇaṃ viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ aññe saṅkhārā 
 puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena 
 saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ aññe saṅkhārā 
 puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena viññāṇañca upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  pe  
  
                  
  
     Sa Pu cakkhāyatanaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena sotāyatanañca upalabbhati

 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe

 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe  dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe

  pesotindriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe

 ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññā vedanā vuttaṃ bhagavā atthi 
 puggalo atta hitāya paṭipanno rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca 
 vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti micchā

 atthipuggalo attahitāya paṭipanno rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca

 bhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe

 ca vattabbe puggalasmiṃ aññātāvindriyanti micchā  pe  
  
     Pa Pu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti

 Lakkhaṇayuttikathā  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati upalabbhati puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭiññā puggalo upalabbhati upalabbhati kehici puggalo kehici na puggaloti  
 Sa Anu puggalo kehici upalabbhati kehici na upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo saccikaṭṭho saccikaṭṭho puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭiññā puggalo saccikaṭṭho sacacikaṭṭho kehici puggalo kehici na puggaloti    
                
 Sa Anu puggalo kehici saccikaṭṭho kehici na saccikaṭṭhoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo vijjamāno vijjamāno puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭiññā puggalo vijjamāno vijjamāno kehici puggalo kehici na puggaloti  
 Sa Anu puggalo kehici vijjamāno Kehici na vijjamānoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
  
                  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo saṃvijjamāno saṃvijjamāno puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭiññā puggalo saṃvijjamāno saṃvijjamāno kehici puggalo kehici na puggaloti  
 Sa Anu puggalo kehici saṃvijjamāno kehici na saṃvijjamānoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
     Sa Pu puggalo atthi atthi puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭiññā puggalo atthi atthi kehici puggalo kehici na puggaloti  
 Sa Anu puggalo kehici atthi kehici natthiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo atthi atthi na sabbo puggaloti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu puggalo natthi natthi na sabbo puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
 Vacanasodhanaṃ

 ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāteti

 Sa Pu puggaloti vā jīvoti vā jīvoti vā puggaloti vā puggalaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se   
 Ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjajateti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Pu añño kāyo añño puggaloti

 Sa Anu aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti

 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
        
   Ucchinno       
   Ese ese   pu  
                  
  
 Anu ha hañci kāyoti vā sarīranti vā sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se 
 ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte Puggaloti vā jīvoti vā jīvoti puggaloti vā puggalaṃ 
 appiyaṃ karitvā ese                  se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte añño 
 kāyo añño puggalo  
  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti  
  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho kāyoti vā sarīranti vā sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ 
 appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte puggaloti vā jīvoti vā jīvoti vā 
 puggaloti vā puggalaṃ appiyaṃ karitvāese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte añño kāyo 
 añño puggalo no ca vattabbe aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti micchā  
 Paṭi ha no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti  
  
 Paṭi Pā no ca vata re vattabbe kāyoti vā sarīranti vā sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ 
 karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte puggaloti vā jīvoti vā jīvoti vā puggaloti 
 vā puggalaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte añño kāyo añño 
 puggaloti  
  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho kāyotivā sarīranti vā sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ 
 appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte puggaloti vā jīvoti vā jīvoti vā 
 puggaloti vā puggalaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte añño kāyo 
 añño puggalo no ca vattabbe aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti micchā  pe  
  
                    
  
 Pa Pu kāyoti vā sarīranti vā sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe 
 same samabhāge tajjāteti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Pu vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipannoti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Pu añño kāyo añño puggaloti  
 Sa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 Pa Paṭikammaṃ ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
 Anu ha hañci kāyoti vā sarīranti vā sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se 
 ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe añaño kāyo añño puggaloti Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi 
 vattabbe kho kāyoti vā sarīranti vā sarīranti vākāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se 
 ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte vuttaṃ bhagavatā                  atthi

 karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya 
 paṭipannoti

 Paññattānuyogo

 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 lokanti

 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 manussabhuto svāyaṃ svāyaṃ sandhāvatīti micchā  pe

 mahiso   Hotīti

 mahiso añño manussabhuto svevāyaṃ sandhāvatīti micchā  pe

     Sa Pu sveva puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti

 Sa Anu hatthacchinno hatthacchinnoca hoti pādacchinno pādacchinnoca hoti 
 hatthapādacchinno hatthapādacchinnoca hoti Kaṇṇacchinno  pe nāsacchinno 
  pekaṇṇanāsacachinno  pe  aṅgulicchinno  pe  aḷacchinno  pe  kaṇḍaracchinno  pe  
 kuṇihatthako  pe  kuṭṭhiyo  pegaṇdhiyo  pekilāsiyo  pe  sosiyo  pe  apamāriyo  peoṭṭho 
  pegoṇo  pe  gadrabho  pe  sūkaro  pemahiso mahisova hotīti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ sveva puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā 
 imaṃ lokanti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā                   
 Pa Pu nanu sotāpanto puggalo manussalokā cuto devalokaṃ upapanno tatthapi 
 sotāpannoca hotīti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa ha hañci sotāpānno puggalo manussalokā vuto devalokaṃ upapanno tatthapi 
 sotāpannoca hoti  
 Pa Pā tena vata re vattabbe sveva puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā 
 imaṃ lokanti  
 Sa Anu sotāpanno puggalo manussalokā cuto devalokaṃ upapanno tatthapi sotāpannoca 
 hotīti katvā tena ca kāraṇena sveva puggalovdhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā 
 imaṃ lokānti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Pu sotāpanno puggalo manussalokā cuto devalokaṃ upapanno tatthapi manusso hotīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu sveva puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
                  
  
 Sa Pu anañño avigato sandhāvatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Pu anañño avigato savadhāvatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Pu hatthacchinno hatthacchinnova hoti pādācchinno pādacchinnova hoti 
 hthapādacchinno hatthapādacchinnova hoti Kannacchinno  pe  nāsacchinno 
  pe kaṇṇanāsacchinno  peaṅgulicchinno  pe  aḷacchinno 
  pekaṇḍaracchinno pekuṇihatthako  pe  phaṇahatthako  pekuṭṭhiyo  pe  gaṇḍiyo 
  pekilāsiyo  pe  sosiyo  pe  apamāriyo  pe  oṭṭhā  pegoṇo  pegaidrako  pe  sūkaro  pe  
 mahiso mahisova hotīti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu sveva puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Pu sarūpo savdhavatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
 Sa Pu sarūpo savdhāvatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Pu taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīranti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
 Sa Pu savedano  pe  sasañño  pe  sasaṅkhāro  pesaviññāṇo sandhāvatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Pu saviññāṇo savdhāvatīti                   
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Pu taṃ jīvaṃ taṅ sarīranti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 Sa Pu viññāṇaṃ sandhāvatīti

 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 Sa Anu vedanā  pe  saññā  pe  saṅkhārā  pe  viññāṇaṃ na sandhāvatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Pu viññāṇaṃ na sandhāvatīti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
  
  Khandhesu bhijjamānesu 
 So ce bhijjati puggalo 
 Ucchedā bhavati diṭṭhi 
 Yā buddhena vivajjitā  
 Khandhesu bhijjamānesu 
 No ce bhijjati puggalo  
 Puggalo sassato hoti  
 Nibbānena samasamoti  
  
 Gati anuyogo  
  
                    
  
     Sa Pu rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññattīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā

 virāgadhammaṃ nirodhadhammaṃ vipariṇāmadhammanti

 khayadhammo vayadhammo virāgadhammo nirodhadhammo vipariṇāmadhammoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Vedanaṃ upādāya  pe  saññaṃ upādāya  pe  saṅkhāre upādāya  pe viññāṇaṃ upādāya 
 puggalassa paññattīti

   Dhammadhātuṃ   machasaṃ syā sīmu  
   Bāvīsatīnaṃ   sabbattha  
  
                    
  
 Pa Anu pañcavokārabhave pañceva puggalāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
                   
     Sa Pu yathā rukkhaṃ upādāya chāyāya paññatti evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa 
 paññattīti  
 Yathā rukkhaṃ upādāya chāyāya paññatti rukkhopi anicco chāyāpi aniccā evamevaṃ 
 rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññatti rūpampi aniccaṃ puggalopi aniccoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Pu yathā rukkhaṃ upādāya chāyāya paññatti añño rukkho aññā chāyā evamevaṃ 
 rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññatti aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
  
     Sa Pu yathā gāmaṃ upādāya gamikassa paññatti evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa 
 paññattīti  
 Yathā gāmaṃ upādāya gamikassa paññatti añño gāmo añño gamiko evamevaṃ rūpaṃ 
 upādāya puggalassa paññatti aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu yathā raṭṭhaṃ upādāya rañño paññatti evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa 
 paññattīti  
 Yathā raṭṭhaṃ upādāya rañño paññatti aññaṃ raṭṭhaṃ añño rājā evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya 
 puggalassa paññatti aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu yathā na nigaḷo negaḷiko yassa nigaḷo so negaḷiko evamevaṃ na rūpaṃ rūpavā 
 yassa rūpaṃ so rūpavāti  
 Yathā na nigaḷo negaḷiko yassa nigaḷo so negaḷiko añño nigaḷo añño negaḷiko evamevaṃ 
 na rūpaṃ rūpavā yassa rūpā so rūpavā aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño rūpavāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
                    
  
     Sa Pu citte citte puggalassa paññattīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Vanu citte citte puggalo jāyati jīyati mīyati cavati upapajjatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Pu dutiye cite uppanne na vattabbo soti vā aññoti vāti                   
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu dutiye cite uppanne na vattabbaṃ kumārakoti vā kumārikāti vāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā vattabbaṃ  
 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ Anu ha hañci dutiye cite uppanne na vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti 
 vā  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe dutiye cite uppanne na vattabbaṃ kumārakotivā kumārikāti 
 vāti  
 Anu A yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti 
 vā dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ kumārakoti vā kumārikāti vāti micchā  
 Paṭi ha hañci vā pana dutiye citte uppanne vatactabbaṃ kumārakoti vā kumārikāti vā  
 Paṭi Pā tena vata re vattabbe dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ soti vā aññeti vā  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vacattabbe kho dutiye citte uppannena vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti 
 vā dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ kumārakoti vā kumārikāti micchā  
     Sa Pu dutiye cite uppanne na vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti vāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
                     
  
 Sa Anu dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃ itthiti vā purisoti vā gahaṭṭhotivā pabbajitoti 
 vā devoti vā manussoti vāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā vattabbaṃ  
 Sa Ni ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 Anu ha hañci dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbasoti vā aññoti vā  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃ devoti vā manussoti vāti  
 Anu Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃsoti vā aññoti vā 
 dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ devoti vā manussoti vāti micchā  
 Paṭi ha hañci vā pana dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ devoti vā manussoti vā  
 Paṭi Pā tena vata re vattabbe dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti vāti  
 Paṭi Ā yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti vā 
 dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ devoti vā manussoti vāti micchā  pe  
  
     Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā                   
 Pa Pu nanu yo passati yaṃ passati yena passati so passati taṃ passati tena passatīti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci yo passati yaṃ passati yena passati so passati taṃ passati tena passati  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
                     
  
     Pa Pu na vattabaṃbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Pu nanu yo suṇāti  pe  yo ghāyati  pe  yo sāyati  pe  yo phūsati  pe  yo vijānāti yaṃ 
 vijānāti yena vijānāti so vijānāti taṃ vijānātitena vijānātīti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci yo vijānāti yaṃ vijānāti yena vijānāti so vijānāti taṃ vijānāti tena vijānāti 
 Anu Pā tena vata                  re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Pu nanu yo na passati yaṃ na passati yena na passati so na passati taṃ na passati 
 tena na passatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci yo na passati yaṃ na passati yena na passati so na passati taṃ na passati 
 tena passati  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
     Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Pu nanu yo na suṇāti  pe  yo na ghāyati  pe  yo na sāyati  pe  yo na phusati  pe  yo na 
 vijānāti yaṃ na vijānāti yena vijānāti so na vijānāti taṃ na vijānāti tena na vijānātīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
                    
  
 Anu ha hañci yo na vijānāti yaṃ na vijānāti yena na vijānāti so na vijānāti taṃ na vijānāti 
 tena na vijānāti  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Pu nanu vuttā bhagavatā  passāmahaṃ bhikkhave dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena 
 atikkantamānusakena satte cavamāne visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte cavamāne 
 uppajjamāne   Hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe sugate duggate yathākammūpage satte 
 pajānāmī ti attheva suttantoti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Niga tena hi puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Sa Pu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  passāmahaṃ bhikkhave dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena 
 atikkantamānusakena satte cavamāne uppajjamāne hīne paṇite suvaṇṇe dubbaṇne sugate 
 duggate yathākammupage satte pajānāmī  ti katvā teneva kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Pu bhagavā dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena rūpā passati puggalaṃ 
 passatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā rūpaṃ passati  
 Sa Anu rūpaṃ puggalo rūpaṃ cavati rūpaṃ uppajjati rūpaṃ yathākammūpaganti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu bhagavā dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena rūpaṃ passati 
 puggalaṃ passatacīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā puggalaṃ passati  
  
      
   Upapajjamāne   machasaṃ  
  
                    
  
 Sa Anu puggalo rūpaṃ rūpāyatanaṃ rūpadhātu nīlaṃ pītakaṃ lohitakaṃ odātaṃ 
 cakkhuviññeyyaṃ cakkhusmiṃ paṭihaññati cakkhussa āpāthaṃ āgacchatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
 Sa Pu bhagavā dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānussakena rūpaṃ passati 
 puggalaṃ passatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā ubho passati sa Anu ubho rūpaṃ rūpāyatanaṃ rūpadhātu ubho nīlā ubho 
 pītakā ubho lohitakā ubho odātā ubho cakkhuviññeyayā                   
 ubho cakkhusmiṃ paṭihaññanti ubho cakkhussa āpāthaṃ āgacchanti ubho cavanti ubho 
 uppajjanti ubo yathākammūpagāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
 Upādāpaññattānuyogo  
     Pa Pu kalyāṇapāpakāni kammāni upalabbhantīti

 kāretā upalabbhatīti

 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu tassa tasseva natthi dukkhassa antakiriyā natthi vaṭṭupacchedo natthi 
 anupādāparinibbānanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 kārenā upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu nibbānaṃ upalabbhatīti nibbānassa kattā kāretā upalabbhatīti

 kāretā upalabbhatīti

 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 kāretā upalabbhatīti

 Sa Anu mahāsamuddo upalabbhatīti mahāsamuddassa kattā kāretā upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu kalyāṇapāpakāni kammāni upalabbhantīti kalyāṇapāpakānaṃ kammānaṃ kattā 
 kāretā upalabbhatīti

 Sa Anu sineru pabbatarājā upalabbhatīti sinerussa pabbatarañño kattā kāretā 
 upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
                    
  
     Sa Pu kalayāṇapāpakāni kammāni upalabbhantīti kalyāṇa pāpakānaṃ kammānaṃ

 Sa Anu āpo upalabbhatīti āpassa kattā kāretā upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 kāretā upalabbhatīti

 Sa Anu tejo upalabbhatīti tejassa kattā kāretā upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 kāretā upalabbhatīti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu vāyo upalabbhatīti vāyassa kattā kāretā upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 kāretā upalabbhatīti

 Sa Anu tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatayo   Upalabbhantīti tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ kattā kāretā 
 upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 kāretā upalabbhatīti

 Sa Anu aññāni kalyāṇapāpakāni kammāni añño kalyāṇapāpakānaṃ kammānaṃ kattā 
 kāretāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vantabbe  pe

 paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aññaṃ āpāyikaṃ dukkhaṃ añño āpāyikassa dukkhassa paṭisaṃvedīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 Sa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu paraṃ kataṃ sukhadukkhanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 kāretā vipākapaṭisaṃvedī upalbhatīti  
                   
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā

 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu sayaṃ katañca paraṃ katañca sukhadukkhanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 kāretā vipākapaṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā

 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 kāretā vipākapaṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti

 Sa Pu so karoti so paṭisaṃvedeti añño karoti añño paṭisaṃvedeti so ca aññoca karonti so 
 ca añño ca paṭisaṃvedenti neva so karoti na so paṭisaṃvedeti na añño karoti na añño 
 paṭisaṃvedetīti

 Kalyāṇavaggo paṭhamo  
  
                    
  
     Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti Sa Paṭiññā 
 āmantā Pa Anu nanu atthi koci iddhiṃ vikubbatīti     
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā Anu ha hañci atthi koci iddhiṃ vikubbati  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
                   
     Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti Sa Paṭiññā 
 āmantā Pa Anu nanu atthi koci dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti  pe  
 Paracittaṃ jānāti    Pe  pubbenivāsaṃ anussarati  pe  
 Dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati  pe  āsavānaṃ khayaṃ  
 Sacchikarotīti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā Anu ha hañci atthi koci āsavānaṃ khayaṃ sacchikaroti  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati  
 Saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti 
  
     Sa Pu atthi koci iddhiṃ vikubbatīti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu yo iddhiṃ vikubbati sveva pugga yo iddhiṃ  
 Na vikubbati na so puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
  
     Sa Pu yo dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddhaṃ suṇati  pe  
 Yo paracittaṃ jānāti  pe  yo pubbenivāsaṃ  
 Anussarati  pe  yo dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati  pe yo āsavānaṃ khayaṃ sacchikaroti 
 sveva puggalo yo  
 Āsavānaṃ khayaṃ na sacchikaroti na so puggaloti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

    P     
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
                    
  
 Sa Niga vuttaṃ bhagavatā  tiṇimāni bhikkhave saṅkhatassa saṅkhatalakkhanāni 
 saṅkhatānaṃ bhikkhave dhammānaṃ uppādo paññāyati vayo paññāyati ṭhitānaṃ   
 Aññathattaṃ paññāyatī ti Puggalassa uppādo paññāyāti vayo paññāyati ṭhitassa 
 aññathattaṃ paññāyati Tena hi puggalo saṅkhatoti  
     Sa Pu puggalassa na uppādo paññāyati na vayo paññāyati na ṭhitassa aññathattaṃ 
 paññāyatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu puggalo asaṅkhatoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
 Sa Niga Vuttaṃ bhagavatā  tiṇimāni bhikkhave asaṅkhatassa asaṅkhatalakkhaṇāni 
 asaṅkhatānaṃ bhikkhave dhammānaṃ na uppādo paññāyati na vayo paññāyati na ṭhitānaṃ 
 aññathattaṃ paññāyatī ti Puggalassa na uppādo paññāyāti na vayo paññāyati naṭhitassa 
 aññathattaṃ paññāyati Tena hi puggalo asaṅkhatoti  
  
     Sa Pu parinibbuto puggalo atthatthamhi natthatthamhīti Atthatthamhiti parinibbuto 
 puggalo sassatoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe pe  
 Sa Anu natthatthamhīti parinibbuto puggalo ucchinnoti Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
  
 Sacchikaṭṭhasabhāvānuyogo  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo kiṃ nissāya tiṭṭhatīti  Bhavaṃ nissāya tiṭaṭhatīti  
 Bhavo anicco saṅkhato paṭiccasamuppanno khayadhammo vayadhammo virāgadhammo 
 nirodhadhammo vipariṇāmadhammoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
         
   hitassa   sīmu  
  
     
  
 Sa Anu puggalopi anicco saṅkato paṭiccasamuppanno khayadhammo vayadhammo 
 virāgadhammo nirodhadhammo vipariṇāmadhammoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe pe  
  
     Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu atthi koci sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ sukhaṃ vedanaṃ 
 vediyāmīti pajānātīti  
                   
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci atthi koci sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti 
 pajānāti  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu atthi koci dukkhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno  pe  
 Adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti 
 pajānātīti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci atthi koci adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno 
 Adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānāti  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Sa Pu  atthi koci sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ  
 Vediyāmīti pajānātī  ti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu yo sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānāti sveva 
 puggalo yo sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmano sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti na pajānāti na so 
 puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe   
  
                    
  
 Sa Anu yo dukkhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno  pe  yo adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno 
 adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānāti sveva puggalo yo adukkhamasukhaṃ 
 vedanaṃ vediyamāno adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti na pajānati na so puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu atthi koci sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānātīti 
 katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭha paramatthenāti Pa Paṭiññā 
 āmantā Sa Anu aññā sukhā vedanā añño sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ 
 vediyāmīti pajānātīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe sa Anu aññā dukkhā                   
 Vedanā  pe  aññā adukakhamasukhā vedanā añño adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ 
 vediyamāno adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānātīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu atthi koci kāye kāyānupassī viharītīti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci atthi koci kāye kāyānupassī viharati  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu atthi koci vedanāsu  pe  citte  pe  dhammesu dhammānupassī viharatīti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
                    
  
 Anu ha hañci atthi koci dhammānupassī viharatī  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
     Sa Pu atthi koci kāye kāyānupassī viharatīti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo 
 upalabbhati saccikaṭṭha paramatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu yo kāye kāyānupassī viharati sveva puggalo yo na kāye kāyānupassī viharati na 
 so puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu yo vedanāsu  pe  citte  pe  dhammesu dhammānupassī 
 Viharati sveva puggalo yo na dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati na so puggaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu atthi koci kāye kāyānupassī viharatīti katvā tena ca  
 Kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu añño kāyo añño kāye kāyānupassī viharatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
                   
 Sa Anu aññā vedanā  pe  aññaṃ cittaṃ  pe  aññe dhammā  
 Añño dhammesu dhammānupassī viharatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Pa Pu puggalo nūpalabbhati   Saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
        
   Upalabbhati   sīmu machasaṃ syā      
  
                    
  
 Pa Anu nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
  Suññato lokaṃ avkkhessu 
 Mogharājā   Sadā sato  
 Attānudiṭṭhiṃ ūhacca    
 Evaṃ maccutaro siyā  
 Evaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ 
 Maccurājā na passatī  ti  
 Attheva suttantoti  
  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Niga tena hi   Puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo avkkhetīti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu saha rūpena avkkheti   vinā rūpena avekkhatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā saha rūpena avekkhati  
 Sa Anu taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīranti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Anu saha rūpena avekkhati vinā rūpena avekkhatīti   Pa Paṭiññā vinā rūpena 
 avekkhati  
 Sa Anu aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo avekkhatīti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu abbhantaragato avekkhati bahiddhā nikkhamitvā avekkhatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā abbhantaragato avekkhati  
 Sa Anu taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīranti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe

 Pa Paṭiññā bahiddhā nikkhamitvā avekkhati  
 Sa Anu aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti

 Pa Anu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno ti 
 Attheva suttantoti

 āmantā

 Anaññathavādīti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  ekapuggalo bhikkhave loke  
 Uppajjamāno uppajjati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya  
 Lokānukampāya atthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanussāna nti 
 Attheva suttantoti

 Pa Niga tena hi puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti

 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
                     
  
 Sa Anu nanu bhagavā saccavādī kālavādī bhūtavādī tathavādī 
 Avitathavādī anaññathavādīti Pa Paṭi āmantā  
 Sa Anu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  sabbe dhammā anattā ti  
 Atthava suttantoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā Sa Nigā tena hi na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati 
 Saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
     Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
                   
 Sa Anu nanu bhagavā saccavādī kālavādī bhūtavādī tathavādī avitathavādī 
 Anaññathavādīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  dukkhameva uppajjamānaṃ uppajjati  
 Dukkhameva nirujjhamānaṃ nirujjhatīti na kaṅkhati na  
 Vicikicchati aparappaccayañāṇamevassa ettha hoti Ettāvatā 
 Kho kaccāna sammādiṭṭhi hotī ti attheva suttantoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Niga tena hi na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabapbhati  
 Saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu nanu vajirā bhikkhunī māraṃ pāpimantaṃ etadavoca  
  Kinnu sattoti paccesi 
 Māra diṭṭhigatannu te  
 Suddhasaṅkhārapuñjoyaṃ nayidha sattupalabbhati  
 Yathāhi aṅgasambhārā hoti saddo ratho iti evaṃ khandhesu santesu 
 Hoti sattoti sammuti     
  
 Dukkhameva hi sambhoti  
 Dukkhaṃ tiṭṭhati veti ca  
 Nāññatra dukkhā sambhoti  
 Nāññaṃ dukkhā nirujjhatī ti  
 Attheva suttantoti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā Sa Niga tena hi na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati

   Sammati   syā  
  
                     
  
     Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu nanu āyasmā ānando bhagavantaṃ etadavoca  
  
                   
  Suñño loko suñño lokoti bhante vuccati  
 Kittāvatā nu kho bhante suñño lokoti vuccatīti  
 Yasmā kho ānanda suññaṃ attena vā attaniyena vā tasmā suñño lokoti vuccati 
 Kiñcānanda suññaṃ 
 Attena vā attaniyena vā  Cakkhuṃ   Kho ānanda  
 Suññaṃ attena vā attaniyena vā Rūpā suññā  pe  
 Cakkhuviññāṇaṃ suññaṃ  pecakkhusamphasso suñño pe  
 Yampidaṃ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṃ sukhaṃ vā  
 Dukakhaṃ vā adukkhamasukhaṃ vā tampi suññaṃ attena vā 
 Attaniyena vā Sotaṃ suññaṃ  pesaddā suññā  pe  
 Sotasamphasso suñño  pe  ghānaṃ suññaṃ  pe  
 Gandhā suññā  pe  jivhā suññā  perasā suññā  pekāyo suñño  pe  phoṭṭhabbā suññā  pe  
 Mano suñño  pe  dhammā suññā  pemanoviññāṇaṃ suññaṃ  pemanosamphasso suñño  pa  
 yampidaṃ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṃ sukhaṃ vā dukkhaṃ vā 
 adukkhamasukhaṃ vā tampi suññaṃ attena vā attaniyena vā Yasmā kho ānanda suññaṃ 
 attena vā attaniyena vā tasmā suñño lokoti  
 Vuccatī ti Attheva suttantoti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā

   Cakkhu    P T S  
  
                    
 Sa Anu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  attani vā bhikkhave sati attaniyaṃ meti assāti  Evaṃ bhante 
 attaniye vā bhikkhave sati attā 
 Meti assāti  Evaṃ bhante Attani ca bhikkhave attaniye  
 Va saccato thetato anupalabbhiyamāne yampidaṃ   Diṭaṭhiṭṭhānaṃ so loko so attā so 
 pecca bhavissāmi nicco dhuvo sassato aviparināmadhammo  
 Sassatisamaṃ tatheva ṭhassāmīti natvāyaṃ bhikkhave kevalo paripūro bāladhammoti  
 Kiñca   No siyā bhante kevalo hi bhante paripūro bāladhammo ti attheva  
 Suttantoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Niga tena hi na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati 
 Saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu nanu bhagavā sāccavādī kālavādī bhūtavādī tathavādī avitathavādī 
 Anāññathavādīti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  tayome seniya satthāro santo 
 Saṃvijjamānā lokasmiṃ Katame tayo idha seniya  
 Ekacco satthā diṭṭheva dhamema attānaṃ saccato thetato paññāpeti abhisamparāyañca attāṃ 
 saccato 
 Thetato paññāpeti Idha pana seniya ekacco satthā diṭṭheva hi kho dhamme attānaṃ saccato 
 thetato  
 Paññāpeti no ca kho abhisamparāyaṃ attānaṃ saccato 
 Thetato paññāpeti Idha pana seniya ekacco satthā diṭṭhe ceva dhamme attānaṃ saccato 
 thetato na paññāpeti Abhisamparāyañca attānaṃ saccato thetato na paññāpeti Tatra seniya  
 Yvāyaṃ satthā diṭṭheveva dhamme attānaṃ saccato  
 Thetato paññāpeti abhisamparāyañca attānaṃ saccato thetato paññāpeti ayaṃ vuccataṃ 
 seniya satthā  
 Sassanavādo Tatra seniya  
  
        
   Yamidaṃ   syā  
   Kiñci   machasaṃ 
  
                    
  
 Yvāyaṃ satthā diṭṭheva hi kho dhamme attānaṃ saccato 
 Thetato paññāpeti no ca kho abhisamparāyaṃ attānaṃ saccato thetato paññāpeti ayaṃ 
 vuccati seniya satthā 
 Ucchedavādo Tatra seniya yvāyaṃ satthā diṭṭhe ceva 
 Dhamme attānaṃ saccato thetato na paññāpeti abhisamparāyañca attānaṃ saccato thetato na 
 paññāpeti  
 Ayaṃ vuccati seniya satthā sammāsambuddho Ime kho  
 Seniya tayo satthāro santo saṃvijjamānā lokasmi nti Attheva suttantoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Niga tena hi na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
     Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu nanu bhagavā saccavādī kālavādī bhūtavādī tathavādī avitathavādī 
 Anaññathavādīti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu vuttaṃ hetaṃ bhagavatā sappikumbhoti Pa Paṭiññā                   
  
 Āmantā  
 Sa Anu atthi koci sappissa kumbhaṃ karotīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe pe  
 Sa Niga tena hi na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati  
 Saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
     Sa Pu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu nanu bhagavā saccavādī kālavādī bhūtavādī tathavādī 
 Avitathavādī anaññathavādīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
                    
  
 Sa Anu vuttaṃ hetaṃ bhagavatā telakumbho  pe  madhukumbho  pe pāṇitakumbho  pe  
 khīrakumbho  pe  udakakumbho  pe  
 Pāniyathālakaṃ  pe  pāniyakosakaṃ  pe  pānīyasarāvakaṃ

 Parihānikathā 
  
   Sa Pu paribhāyati arahā arahattāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā sa Anu sabbattha arahā arahattā parihāyatīti
