 Samannāgato  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
    Sa Pu na vattabbaṃ arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno  
 Puggalo tīhi phalena samannāgatoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Pa Anu nanu arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena puggalena  
 Tihī phalāni paṭiladdhāni tehi ca aparihīnoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
  
                    
 Anu ha hañci arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena 
 Puggalena tiṇi phalāni paṭiladdhāni tehi ca aparihīno  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe arahattasacchikiriyāya 
 Paṭipanenā puggalo tīhi phalehi samnnāgatoti  
  
    Pu Pu na vattabbaṃ anagāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno 
 Puggalo dvīhi phalehi samannāgatoti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena 
 Puggalena                   dve   phalāni paṭiladdhāni tehi ca aparihīnoti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Anu ha hañci anāgāmipalasacchikariyāya paṭipannena 
 Puggalena dve phalāni paṭiladdhāni te hi ca 
 Aparihīno  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe anāgāmiphaḷasacchikiriyāya 
 Paṭipanno puggalo dvīhi phalehi samannāgatoti  
  
     Pu Pu na vattabbaṃ sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno 
 Puggalo sotāpattiphalena samannāgatoti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena 
 Puggalena sotapattiphalaṃ paṭiladdhaṃ te na ca aparihīnoti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Anu ha hañci sakadāgāmiphalasacchikariyāya paṭipannena 
 Puggalena sotāpattiphalaṃ paṭiladdhaṃ te na ca 
 Aparihīno  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya 
 Paṭipanno puggalo sotāpattiphalena samannāgatoti  
  
    Sa Pu arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena puggalena 
 Tiṇi phalāni paṭiladdhāni tehi ca aparihīnoti 
 Arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo tīhi 
 Phalehi samannāgatoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
   Devava   sīmu 
  
                    
 Sa Anu arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena puggalena 
 Cattāro maggā paṭiladdhā tehi ca aparihīnoti 
 Arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo catūhi 
 Maggehi samannāgatoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
    Sa Pu anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena puggalena 
 Dve   phalāni paṭiladdhāni tehi ca aparihīnoti 
 Anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo  
 Dvīhi phalehi samannāgatoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Sa Anu anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena puggalena 
 Tayo maggā paṭiladdhā tehi ca aparihīnoti 
 Anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo tīhi 
 Maggehi samannāgatoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
    Sa Pu sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena puggalena 
 Sotāpattiphalāni paṭiladdhaṃ te na ca aparihīnoti 
                   sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo 
 Sotāpattiphalena samannāgatoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 Sa Anu sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannena puggalena 
 Dve maggā paṭiladdhā tehi ca aparihīnoti 
 Sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo 
 Dvīhi maggehi samannāgatoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
 Aparāpi samannāgatakathā niṭṭhitā 
  
   Adavava   sīmu  
  
                    
      Saññojanappahāna kathā  
   Sa Pu sabbasaññojanānaṃ pāhānaṃ arahattanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu arahattamaggena sabbe saññojanā pahiyantīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu arahattamaggena sabbe saññojanā pahiyantiti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu arahattamaggena sakkāyadiṭṭhiṃ vicikicchā sīlabbataparāmāsaṃ pajahatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu arahattamaggena sakkāyadiṭṭhiṃ vicikicchā sīlabbataparāmāsaṃ pajahatīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu nanu tiṇṇaṃ saññojanānaṃ pahānaṃ sotāpattaphalaṃ 
 Vuttaṃ bhagavatāti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Anu ha hañci tiṇṇaṃ saññojanānaṃ pahānaṃ sotāpattiphalaṃ 
 Vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe arahattamaggena 
 Sabbe saññojanā pahiyantīti  
  
   Sa Pu arahattamaggena sabbe saññojanā pahiyantiti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu arahattamaggena oḷārikaṃ kāmarāgaṃ oḷārikaṃ 
 Vyāpādaṃ pajahatiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
                    
                    
   Sa Pu arahattamaggena oḷārikaṃ kāmarāgaṃ oḷārikaṃ 
 Vyāpādaṃ pajahatiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu nanu kāmarāgavyāpādānaṃ tanubhāvaṃ sakadāgamiphalaṃ 
 Vuttaṃ bhagavāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Anu ha hañci kāmarāgavyṛpādānaṃ tanubhāvaṃ sakadāgāmiphalaṃ 
 Vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabeba arahattamaggena 
 Sabbe saññojanā pahīyantiti  
  
   Sa Pu arahattamaggena sabbe saññojanā pahiyantiti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu arahattamaggena aṇusahagataṃ kāmarāgaṃ 
 Aṇusahagataṃ vyāpādaṃ pajahatiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu arahattamaggena aṇusahagataṃ kāmarāgaṃ aṇusahagataṃ vyāpādaṃ pajahatiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu nanu kāmarāgavyāpādānaṃ anavasesappahānaṃ 
 Anāgāmiphalaṃ vuttaṃ bhagavatāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Anu ha hañci kāmarāgavyāpādānaṃ anavasesappahānaṃ 
 Anāgāmiphalaṃ vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe  arahattamaggena 
 Sabbe saññojanā pahiyanti ti  
  
   Sa Pu arahattamaggena sabbe saṃyojanā pahiyantiti   
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
  
                    
 Sa Anu nanu rūparāgaarūparāgamānauddhaccaavijjāya 
 Anavasesappahānaṃ arahattaṃ vuttaṃ bhagavatāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ṭha hañci rūparāgaarūparāgamānauddhaccaavijjāya 
 Anavasesappahānaṃ arahattaṃ vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe  arahattamaggena 
 Sabbe saññojanā pahiyanti ti  
  
   Sa Pu na vattabbaṃ sabbe saṃyojanā pahānaṃ arahattanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Pa Anu nanu arahato sabbe saññojanā pahīnāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā                    
 Anu ṭha hañci arahato sabbe saññojanā pahīnā  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe  sabbasaññojanānaṃ 
 Pahānaṃ arahatta nti  
 Saññojanappahānakathā niṭṭhitā  
 Catuttho vaggo niṭṭhito  
  
 Tassa uddānaṃ  
 Gihissa arahā saha upapattiyā arahā Arahato 
 Sabbe dhammā anāsavā Arahā catūhi phalehi 
 Samannāgato evamevaṃ   jahi upekkhāhi  
 Bodhiyā buddho lakkhaṇa   samannāgato 
 Bodhisatto    okkantiniyāmo caritabrahmacariyo  
 Paṭipannako phalena samannāgato  
 Sabbasaññojanānaṃ pahānaṃ arahattanti  
  
   Evameva         Salakkhaṇa   sīmu   Potthakesu natthi  
  
                    
                    
 Pañcamo vaggo 
     Vimuttikathā 
  
   Sa Pu vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu yaṃ kiñci vimuttiñāṇaṃ sabbaṃ taṃ vimuttanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu paccavekkhaṇañāṇaṃ vimuttanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
   Sa Pu vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu gotrabhuno puggalassa vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa  
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttanti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sotāpannassa ñāṇaṃ sotāpattiphalaṃ pattassa 
 Paṭiladdhassa adhigatassa sacchikatassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
                    
   Sa Pu sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa  
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttanti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sakadāgāmissa ñāṇaṃ sakadāgāmiphalaṃ pattassa 
 Paṭiladdhassa adhigatassa sacchikatassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa  
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttanti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu anāgāmissa ñāṇaṃ anāgāmiphalaṃ pattassa 
 Paṭiladdhassa adhigatassa sacchikatassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa  
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttanti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
                   sa Anu arahato ñāṇaṃ arahattaṃ pattassa paṭiladdhassa 
 Adhigatassa sacchikatassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sotāpattiphalasamaṅgissa paṭipannassa puggalassa vimuttiñāṇaṃ 
 Vimuttanti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sotāpantiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimutatanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sakadāgāmiphalasamaṅgissa paṭipannassa puggalassa vimuttiñāṇaṃ 
 Vimuttanti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimutatanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
    Sa Pu anāgāmiphalasamaṅgissa puggalassa vimuttiñāṇaṃ 
 Vimuttanti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimutatanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
                    
    Sa Pu arahattaphalasamaṅgissa puggalassa vimuttiñāṇaṃ 
 Vimuttanti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimutatanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
    Sa Pu sotāpattiphalasamaṅgissa puggalassa vimuttiñāṇaṃ 
 Vimuttataṃ taṃ ca phalaṃ   pattassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sotāpantiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimutataṃ taṃ ca phalaṃ pattassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
    Sa Pu sakadāgāmiphalasamaṅgissa puggalassa vimuttiñāṇaṃ 
 Vimuttanaṃ taṃ ca phalaṃ   pattassa ñāṇanti                    
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimutataṃ taṃ ca phalaṃ pattassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
    Sa Pu anāgāmiphalasamaṅgissa puggalassa vimuttiñāṇaṃ 
 Vimuttataṃ taṃ ca phalaṃ   pattassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimutataṃ taṃ ca phalaṃ pattassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
    Sa Pu arahattaphalasamaṅgissa puggalassa vimuttiñāṇaṃ 
 Vimuttanaṃ taṃ ca phalaṃ   pattassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu arahattasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimutataṃ taṃ ca phalaṃ pattassa ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
 Vimutatikathā niṭṭhitā 
  
   Vimuttañca phalaṃ   machasaṃ  
  
                    
     Asekhañāṇakathā 
   Sa Pu sekhassa asekhañāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sekho asekhaṃ dhammaṃ jānāti passati diṭṭhaṃ 
 Viditaṃ sacchikataṃ upasampajja viharati kāyena 
 Phusitvā viharatīti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
 Sa Anu nanu sekho asekhaṃ dhammaṃ na jānāti  
 Na passati adiṭṭhaṃ aviditaṃ asacchikataṃ 
 Na usampajja viharati na kāyena phusitvā viharatīti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
  
 Anu ha hañci sekho asekhaṃ dhammaṃ na jānāti  
 Na passati adiṭṭhaṃ aviditaṃ asacchikataṃ 
 Na upasampajja viharati na kāyena phusitvā na viharatiti  
  
  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe sekhassa asekhaṃ 
 Ñāṇaṃ atthiti                    
  
   Sa Pu asekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi asekho asekhaṃ dhammaṃ jānāti passati viditaṃ 
 Sacchikataṃ upasampajja viharati kāyena 
 Phusitvā viharatīti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi sekho asekhaṃ 
 Dhammaṃ jānāti passati diṭṭhaṃ 
 Viditaṃ sacchikataṃ upasampajja viharati kāyena 
 Phusitvā viharatīti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
                    
   Sa Pu sekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi sekho asekhaṃ 
 Dhammaṃ na jānāti na passati adiṭṭhaṃ 
 Aviditaṃ asacchikataṃ na upasampajja viharati na kāyena 
 Phusitvā viharatīti  
  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu asekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi asekho asekhaṃ 
 Dhammaṃ na jānāti na passati adiṭṭhaṃ 
 Aviditaṃ asacchikataṃ na upasampajja viharati na kāyena 
 Phusitvā viharatīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sekhassa asekha ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu gotrabhuno puggalassa sotāpattimagge ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
 Sa Anu sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Sotāpattiphale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Anu sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya  peanāgāmi 
 Phalasacchikiriyāya  pe  arahattasacchikiriyāya 
 Paṭipannassa puggalassa arahatte ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ sekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi ti  
 Sa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu ayasmā ānando sekho  bhagavā 
 Uḷāro ti jānāti  Sāriputto thero mahā 
 Moggallāno thero uḷāro ti jānātīti  
 Sa Paññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci āyasmā anando sekho  bhagavā 
 Uḷāro ti jānāti                    sāriputto thero  
 Mahāmoggallāno thero uḷāro ti jānāti  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sekhassa asekhaṃ 
 Ṇāṇaṃ atthiti  
  
 Asekhañāṇakathā niṭṭhitā  
  
                    
     Viparitakathā  
   Sa Pu paṭhavikasiṇa   samāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu anicce niccanti vipariyesoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Anu dukkhe sukhanti  pe  anattani attāti  pe  
 Asubhe subhanti vipariyesoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu akasalanti 
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Anu nanu kusalanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci kusalaṃ  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe paṭhavikasiṇasamapattiṃ 
 Samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇanti  
  
   Paṭhavikasiṇaṃ   syā pathavikasiṇaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
   Sa Pu anicce niccanti vipariyeso So ca akusaloti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇaṃ taṃ ca akusalanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Pu dukkhe sukhanti  pe  anattani attāti  pe  
 Asubhe subhanti vipariyeso so ca akusaloti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇaṃ tañca akusalanti 
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
                    
   Sa Pu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇaṃ taṃ ca akusalanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu anicce niccanti vipariyeso so ca kusaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇaṃ taṃ ca akusalanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu dukkhe sukhanti  pe  anattani attāti  pe  
 Asubhe subhanti vipariyeso so ca kusaloti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu arahā paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpajjeyyāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu hañci arahā paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpajjeyya  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ 
 Samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇanti 
  
                    
   Sa Pu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇaṃ arahā 
 paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpajjeyyāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu atthi arahato vipariyesoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu atthi arahato vipariyesoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu atthi arahato saññāvipariyeso cittaviparisoso diṭṭhivipariyesoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu natthi arahato saññāvipariyeso cittaviparisoso diṭṭhivipariyesoti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci natthi arahato saññāvipariyeso cittavipariyeso diṭṭhivipariyeso  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato 
 Vipariyeso ti  
  
    Sa Pu na vattabbaṃ paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa 
 Viparīte ñāṇa nti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā                    
 Pa Anu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpajjattassa sabbeva paṭhavīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Pa Niga tena hi paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa 
 Viparīte ñāṇanti  
  
    Sa Pu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte 
 Ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
   Pathavikasiṇaṃ samāpattiṃ samāpajjantassa   machasaṃ paṭhavikasiṇaṃ samāpattiṃ 
 samāpajjattassa   syā paṭhaviti samāpajjatassa        
                    
 Sa Anu nanu paṭhavī atthi atthi ca koci paṭhaviṃ paṭhavite samāpajjatiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci paṭhavī atthi atthi ca koci paṭhaviṃ paṭhavito 
 Samāpajjati  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe  paṭhavikasiṇā 
 Samāpattiṃ samāpannassa viparīte ñāṇanti  
  
    Sa Pu paṭhavī atthi paṭhaviṃ paṭhavito samāpajjattassa 
 Viparitaṃ hotī ti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu nibbānaṃ atthi nibbānaṃ nibbānato samāpajjattassa 
 Viparitaṃ hotīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Niga tena hi na vattabbaṃ  paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ 
 Samāpattassa viparīte ñāṇanti  
  
 Viparitakathā niṭṭhitā 
  
                    
     Niyāmakathā 
   Sa Pu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu niyatassa aniyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya natthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya natthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti                    
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu niyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu niyatassa niyāmagamanāya natthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya natthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aniyatassa aniyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
                    
   Sa Pu aniyatassa aniyāmagamanāya natthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya natthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi satipaṭṭhānā 
  Pe  sammappadhānā  pe  iddhipādā  peindriyā 
  Pe  balā  pe  bojjhaṅgāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya natthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya natthi niyāmo  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe  aniyatassa niyāgamanāya 
 Atthi ñāṇanti  
  
    Sa Anu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya natthi satipaṭṭhānā 
  Pe  bojjhaṅgāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya natthi bojjhaṅgā  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe  aniyatassa niyāgamanāya 
 Atthi ñāṇanti  
  
                    
    Sa Pu aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā                    
 Sa Anu gotrabhuno puggalassa sotāpattimagge 
 Ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Anu sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Sotāpattiphale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Anu sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya  peanāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya 
  Pe  arahattasacchikiriyāya  
 Paṭipanssa puggalassa arahatte ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
    Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu bhagavā jānāti ayaṃ puggalo sammattaniyāmaṃ 
 Okkamissati bhabbo ayaṃ puggalo 
 Dhammaṃ abhisametunti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci bhagavā jānāti ayaṃ puggalo sammattaniyāmaṃ 
 Okkāmissati bhabbo ayaṃ puggalo 
 Dhammaṃ abhisametunti  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe aniyatassa niyāmagamanāya  
 Atthi ñāṇanti  
  
 Niyāmakathā niṭṭhitā  
  
 Abhisametuṃ   sīmu machasaṃ  
  
                    
     Paṭisambhidākathā 
   Sa Pu sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sammutiñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sammutiñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu ye keci sammutiṃ jānanti paṭisambhidā pattāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
                    
   Sa Pu cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu ye keci paracittaṃ jānanti sabbe te paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu sabbā paññā paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
                    
   Sa Pu sabbaṃ paññā paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa atthi paññā paṭisambhidāti Pa Paṭi na 
 hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Anu apokasiṇaṃ  pe  tejokasiṇaṃ  pe  
 Vāyokasiṇaṃ  pe  nilakasiṇaṃ  pepitakasiṇaṃ  
  Pe  lohitakasiṇaṃ  pe  odātakasiṇaṃ 
  Pe  ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ  peviññāṇañcāyatanaṃ 
  Pe ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ  pe  
 Nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaṃ samāpannassa  pe  
 Dānaṃ dadantassa  pe  cīvaraṃ dadantassa  pe  
 Paṇḍapātaṃ dadantassa  pe  senāsanaṃ dadantassa 
  Pe  gilānapaccayabhesajjaparikkhāraṃ dadanantassa 
 Atthi paññā sā paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Pa Su na vattabbaṃ sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Pa Anu atthi lokuttarā paññā sāpaññā na paṭisambhidāti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Anu Pā tena hi sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidāti  
  
 Paṭisambhidākathā niṭṭhitā  
  
                    
     Sammutiñāṇakathā  
   Sa Pu na vattabbā sammutiñāṇaṃ saccārammaṇaññeva 
 Na aññārammaṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
                   pa Anu nanu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa atthi 
 Ñāṇaṃ paṭhavikasiṇañca sammutisaccamhiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Anu ha hañci paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa atthi 
 Ñāṇaṃ paṭhavikasiṇañca sammutisaccamhi  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sammutiñāṇaṃ 
 Saccārammaṇaññeva na aññārammaṇanti  
  
   Sa Pu na vattabbā sammutiñāṇaṃ saccārammaṇaññeva 
 Na aññārammaṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Pa Anu nanu āpokasiṇaṃ  pe  tejokasiṇaṃ  pe  
 Gilānapaccaya bhesajjaparikkhāraṃ dadantassa atthi 
 Ñāṇaṃ gilānapaccaya besajjaparikkhāro ca 
 Sammutisaccamhiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Anu ha hañci gilānapaccayabhesajjaparikkhāraṃ dadantassa 
 Atthi ñāṇaṃ gilānapaccayabhesajja parikkhāro ca 
 Sammutisaccamhi  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe sammutiñāṇaṃ 
 Saccārammaṇaññeva na aññārammaṇanti  
  
   Sa Pu sammutiñāṇaṃ saccārammaṇaññeva na aññārammaṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Sa Anu tena ñāṇena dukkhaṃ parijānāti Samudayaṃ 
 Pajahati nirodhaṃ sacchikaroti maggaṃ bhāvetīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
 Sammutiñāṇakathā niṭṭhitā  
  
                    
     Cittārammaṇakathā  
   Sa Pu cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññeva 
 Na aññārammaṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Pa Anu nanu atthi koci sarāgaṃ cittaṃ sārāgaṃ 
 Cittanti pajānātīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Anu ha hañci atthi koci sarāgaṃ cittaṃ sarāgaṃ 
 Cittanti pajānāti  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe cetopariyāye 
 Ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññeva na aññārammaṇanti                    
 Sa Anu nanu atthi koci vitarāgaṃ cittaṃ  pesadosaṃ 
 Cittaṃ  pe  vitadosaṃ cittaṃ  pesamohaṃ cittaṃ  pevitahohaṃ cittaṃ  pe  saṅkhittaṃ 
 Cittaṃ  pe  vikkhittaṃ cittaṃ  pe  mahaggataṃ cittaṃ  peamaggahataṃ cittaṃ  pe  sauttaraṃ 
 cittaṃ  pe  anuttaraṃ cittaṃ  pe  samohiṃ cittaṃ  pe  asamāhitaṃ cittaṃ  pevimuttaṃ cittaṃ 
  pe  avimuttaṃ cittaṃ  pe  avimuttaṃ cittaṃnti pajānātīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci atthi koci avimuttaṃ cittaṃ avimuttaṃ 
 Cittanti pajānāti  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe cetopariyāye 
 Ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññeva na aññārammaṇatti  
  
   Sa Pu phassārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ cetopariyāye ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci phassārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe cetopariyāye 
 Ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññeva aññārammaṇanti  
  
                    
   Sa Pu vedanārammane ñāṇaṃ  pe saññārammaṇe 
 Ñāṇaṃ   cetanārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ   cittārammaṇe 
 Ñāṇaṃ   saddhārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ   viriyārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ   sattārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ   
 samādhārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ   paññārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ   rāgārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ   dosārammaṇe 
 ñāṇaṃ   mohārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ   peanottappārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ cotopariyāye 
 ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā 
 Anu ha hañci anottappārammane ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ  
 Cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ  
 Anu Pā no ca vata re vattabbe cetopariyāye 
 Ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññeva na aññārammaṇatti  
  
   Sa Pu phassārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ cetopariyāye ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu phassapariyayāye ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu vedanārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ  pe saññārammaṇo 
 Ñāṇaṃ  pe  anottappārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ na 
 Vattabbaṃ cetopariyāye ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu anottappapariyāye ñāṇanti 
                   pa Paṭi na vehaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññeva 
 Na aññārammaṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu cetopariyāye ñāṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ 
 Cittārammaṇaññeva na aññārammaṇanti  
  
 Cittārammaṇa kathā niṭṭhitā 
  
                    
     Anāgatañāṇakatha 
   Sa Pu anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu anāgataṃ mulato jānāti hetuto jānāti  
 Nidānato jānāti sambhavato jānāti pabhavato 
 Jānāti samuṭṭhānato jānāti āhārato 
 Jānāti ārammaṇato jānāti paccayato 
 Jānāti samudayato jānātīti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthiti Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu anāgataṃ hetupaccayataṃ jānāti ārammaṇapaccayataṃ 
 Jānāti adhipatipaccayataṃ jānāti  
 Anantarapaccayataṃ jānāti samanantarapaccayataṃ jānātīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
  
                    
 Sa Anu gotrabhuno puggalassa sotāpattimagge 
 Ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe 
 Sa Anu sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa 
 Sotāpattiphale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Sa Anu sakadāgāmī  pe  anāgāmi                     paarahattasacchikiriyāya 
 Paṭipannassa puggalassa arahattena ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  pāṭalīputtassa kho 
 Ānanda tayo antarāyā bhavissanti aggito 
 Vā udakato vā mithubhedā vā ti a  attheva 
 Suttanto ti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Niga tena hi anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
  
 Anāgatañāṇakathā niṭṭhitā 
  
  A  dīghanikāya   mahāparinibbāna sutta  
  
                    
     Paccuppannañāṇakathā  
   Sa Pu paccuppanne   ñāṇaṃ atthiti 
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu tena ñāṇena taṃ ñāṇaṃ jānātīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu tena ñāṇena taṃ jānātiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu tena ñāṇena taṃ ñāṇaṃ ñāṇanti jānātiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu tena ñāṇena taṃ ñāṇaṃ ñāṇanti jānātiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu taṃ ñāṇaṃ tassa ñāṇassa ārammaṇanti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu taṃ ñāṇaṃ ñāṇassa ārammaṇanti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu tena phassena taṃ phassaṃ phusati tāya vedanāya 
 Taṃ vedanaṃ vedati tāya saññāya taṃ saññaṃ sañjānāti tāya cetanāya taṃ cetanaṃ 
 Ceteni tena cittena taṃ cittaṃ cintoti  
 Tena vitakkena taṃ vitakkaṃ vitakketi  
 Tena vicārena taṃ vicāraṃ vicāreti Tāya 
 Pītiyā taṃ pītiṃ piyāyati tāya satiyā taṃ 
 Satiṃ sarati tāya paññāya taṃ paññaṃ pajānāti  
   Paṭuppanne   machasaṃ 
  
                    
 Tena khaggena taṃ khaggaṃ chindati tena pharasunā                   taṃ 
 pharasuṃ tacchati tāya kuṭṭārāya taṃ kuṭhāriṃ   tacchati tāya vāsiyā taṃ vāsiṃ tacchati 
 tāya suciyā taṃ suciṃ sibbeti tena aṅgulaggena taṃ aṅgulaggaṃ parāmasati tena nāsikaggena 
 taṃ nāsikaggaṃ parāmasati tena matthakena taṃ matthakaṃ parāmasati tena guthena taṃ 
 guthaṃ dhovati tena muttena taṃ muttaṃ dhovati tena kheḷena taṃ kheḷaṃ dhovati tena 
 pubbena taṃ pubbā dhovati tena lohitena taṃ lohitaṃ dhovatīti  
  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ paccuppanne ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu nanu sabbasaṅkhāro aniccato diṭṭhe tampi 
 Ñāṇaṃ aniccato diṭṭhaṃ hotīti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Anu ha hañci sabbasaṅkhāre aniccato diṭṭhe tampi 
 Ñāṇaṃ aniccato diṭṭhaṃ hoti  
 Anu Pā tena vata re vattabbe paccuppanne ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
  
 Paccuppannañāṇakathā niṭṭhitā  
  
   Kudhāriyā taṃ kudhāriṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Phalañāṇakathā  
   Sa Pu sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu sāvako phalassa kataṃ paññāpetīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu atthi sāvakassa phalaparopariyanti indriyaparopariyanti 
 Puggalaparopariyantīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu atthi sāvakassa khandhapaññatti āyatanapaññatti 
                   dhātupaññatti saccapaññanti indripaññatti 
 Puggalapaññattīti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu sāvako jino satthā sammāsambuddho sabbaññu 
 Sabbadassāvī dhammasāmi dhammapaṭisaraṇoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
   Sa Pu sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Sa Anu sāvako anuppannassa dhammassa uppādetā 
 Asañjātassa maggassa sañjanetā anakkhātassa 
 Maggassa akkhātā maggaññu maggavidu maggakovidoti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
  
                    
   Pa Pu na vattabbaṃ sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
 Pa Paṭiññā āmantā  
 Pa Anu sāmako aññāṇiti  
 Pa Paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe  pe  
 Pa Niga tena hi sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthiti  
  
 Phalañāṇakathā niṭṭhitā  
 Vañcamo vaggo niṭṭhito 
 Mahāpaṇṇāsako  
  
 Tassa uddānaṃ  
 Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttaṃ    sekhassa asekhaṃ   ñāṇaṃ viparīte ñāṇaṃ aniyatassa 
 niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇaṃ sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā sammuti ñāṇaṃ ceto pariyāye 
 ñāṇaṃ āgate ñāṇaṃ paccuppanne ñāṇaṃsāvakaphale ñāṇanti  
  
   Vimutti   sīmu   Asekhe   sīmu
